    SELECT `l`.`list_id`, `l`.`list_name`, `l`.`user_id`, `u`.`user_id` AS `user_id0`, `u`.`date_created`, `u`.`email`, `u`.`password`, `u`.`user_name`, `u`.`user_type`
    FROM `lists` AS `l`
    LEFT JOIN `users` AS `u` ON `l`.`user_id` = `u`.`user_id`
    WHERE `l`.`list_id` = @__listId_0
    LIMIT 1
) AS `t`
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT `t0`.`id`, `t0`.`list_id`, `t0`.`title_id`, `t0`.`UserRating`, `t0`.`Watched`, `t2`.`title_id` AS `title_id0`, `t2`.`cast`, `t2`.`country`, `t2`.`date_added`, `t2`.`description`, `t2`.`director`, `t2`.`duration`, `t2`.`listed_in`, `t2`.`rating`, `t2`.`release_year`, `t2`.`title_name`, `t2`.`type`, `t2`.`user_rating`, `t2`.`watched` AS `watched0`
